SHUGS LDAN 'KHRUL MED RANG YIN 'DUG CES YID CHES BRTAN PO RNYED
PA'I GTAM MANG DU GLENG BAR BYAS, SKU GSOL GYI MDZAD SGO ZIN
'PHRAL DE GA'I TSOMS

CHEN DU BLA SPRUL SKU DRAG ,DGON GYI DGE 'DUN SOGS 'DUS TSOGS
MANG TZAM LA MGON DKAR, RNAM SRAS, TSE RING MA BCAS KYI G-YANG
CHOG SOGS LJAGS LUNG GNANG, BKRAS LHUN DU LAN RJES MA PHEBS PA'I
DUS 'DIR

BSHOS ZAS MI GTZANG BA BYUNG BA LTA BU'I RKYEN LAS GSUS PHO'I
SNYUN GZHI DOS DRAG PA ZHIG GSAR DU BYUNG TSUL BZHES PAR YANG
YANG 'PHAR LDANG GI RNAM PA'ANG LAN 'GA' BYUNG, BAR DU TZONG KHA
LHA KHANG SOGS SU BYON TE BKRAS LHUN

GYI NANG RTEN KHAG ZHIB GZIGS DANG SGRON DAR THUGS SMON SOGS
KYANG GNANG, SKYABS DBYINGS NAS BKRAS BLAS RGYAL CHEN BSTEN
RGYU'I SKOR SOGS LA PHYIN CHAD KYI SPANG BLANG JI LTAR BYA TSUL
RTZA TSIG CIG BKA' RTZOM DGOS TSUL

@205B ZHUS PAR, GONG GSAL LO RGYUS ZHIB 'KHOD THOG ,PHYIN CHAD
ZLA DUS RGYAS BCAD KYIS BSTEN GSOL JI LTAR BYED PA SOGS SPANG
BLANG GI RIM PA SPYI DANG, LHAG PAR GSER SKYEMS KYI RGYU CHANG
GIS MI BYED PAR RGYA JA'I KHU BAS BYA DGOS BA TSUN

'DUL KHRIMS LA RTZIS SU BYED CING, SPYIR BTANG SDOM GSUM GYI
BCAS MTSAMS LEGS PAR BSRUNG BA DANG, YANG SGOS DGE LDAN LTA GRUB
GTZANG MAR 'DZIN CING BSTAN SRUNG GNYAN PO 'DI NYID LA RGYU
MTSAN SHES NAS YID CHES BRTAN

PO BSKYED PA DGOS TSUL RNAMS ZHIB 'KHOD KYI BCA' KHRIMS RTZA
TSIG KYANG GSUNG RTZOM GNANG BA SOGS KHONG PA TSOS GSOL BTAB KYI
DON RNAMS 'PHRAL SMIN MDZAD, NUB CIG MTSAN RMIS SU, RJE NYID
DANG SER SKYA DRAG PA MANG PO LHAN

BZHUGS THOG ,'DUM BSGRIG BYA RGYU YOD ZER MUR, TSOGS MCHOD SER
SGRENG GI HVA SHANG 'DRA BA'I MI GZUGS BONGS CHE BA ZHIG BYUNG
BAR CHOS SKYONG DRAG POS LAN GNYIS SU GZIR BA SOGS KYI LTAS
MTSAN GSAL BAR BYUNG TSUL PHEBS

PA YANG MCHIS, YANG BKRAS BLA NAS ZHUS NGOR DE GA'I G-YANG SGRUB
ZHAL GSO SOGS GNANG RGYUR CHOG GRVAR NOR LHA 'GA'I RJES GNANG
DANG, BUM RDZAS KHAG GI THO LJAGS SGRIGS, GA-YANG CHOG SPYOR
DNGOS RJES GTZANG BCAS GNANG,

BAR SKABS RNAMS SU KUN GZIGS RIN PO CHE'I GZIM CHUNG MJAL KHA
DANG, RTEN GTZO KHAG LA MCHOD SPRIN, DGE 'DUN BSNYEN BKUR SOGS
RGYA CHER MDZAD CING, DZA BLA SOGS KYI SGER SHAG 'GAR YANG SPYAN
DDRANGS PA BZHIN BYON PA

SKYEL PHEBS SKYEL BA SOGS LA BKRA SHIS BDE LEGS KYI SGRON DAR
STZAL BA DANG BCAS DBUS PHYOGS SU CHIBS KHA BSKYOD, LAM

KHEL DU RGYAL RTZE DPAL 'KHOR CHOS SDE BAS GDAN DRANGS PAR TSOGS
CHEN DU CHOS MANG DU GSUNGS SHING, ZHI GNAS GRVA TSANG DU'ANG
DNGUL CHU'I NYIN ZHAG PHRUGS GCIG DANG, SHUGS LDAN GYI BSKANG
CHOG SKOR BCAS KYI LJAGS

LUNG SOGS GNANG, LNGA RIG YONGS LA MKHAS PA'I GRAGS SNYAN CAN
'BI LUNG DGE BSHES NGAG DBANG YON TAN PA MJAL KHAR BCAR BAR LHOD
MJAL GNANG ZHING, SGRA RIG SKOR SOGS KYI GSUNG GLENG 'PHEL, DGE
BSHES

PAS DON LA GNAS PA'I BSTOD BSNGAGS KYI ZHU GSOL 'GA' PHUL BA 'OG
TU 'BYUNG, NO YON BYAMS CHOS NAS BRAG KHUG SGER GZHIS SU GDAN
DRANGS PAR 'BRAS BLO GLING LHO BA DGE BSHES BLO BZANG BSAM GTAN

MA BCAS KYI LJAGS LUNG, DGE BSHES PAS PAn CHEN N'A RO PA SOGS
KYI RDZOGS RIM NYAMS

MGUR 'GA'I DRI BA ZHUS PA'I BKA' LAN MCHAN DANG BCAS PA SOGS
